</th>

<span class="expandline" title="26 more..."><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Scores_featuring_the_cello&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Scores featuring the cello</a></span>;
